\"lib/internal/per_context/primordials.js\", \"symbol\": \"createSafeIterator\"}\n  ],\n  \"text\": \"Node.js core in github.com/nodejs/node defends against prototype pollution through several coordinated mechanisms.\\n\\n## 1. The Primordials System (lib/internal/per_context/primordials.js)\\nThis is the **central defense file**. It captures all JS built-in constructors and methods at startup before user code can mutate them. Key techniques:\\n- **`uncurryThis`**: Binds `Function.prototype.call` before it can be tampered with, used to safely call prototype methods without going through the prototype chain\\n- **`applyBind`**: Same pattern using `Function.prototype.apply`\\n- **`makeSafe(unsafe, safe)`**: Creates subclasses of `Map`, `Set`, `WeakMap`, `WeakSet`, `FinalizationRegistry`, and `WeakRef` with their prototypes set to `null` via `ObjectSetPrototypeOf(safe.prototype, null)` and frozen — producing `SafeMap`, `SafeSet`, `SafeWeakMap`, `SafeWeakSet`, `SafeFinalizationRegistry`, `SafeWeakRef`\\n- **`createSafeIterator`**: Creates safe iterator classes whose prototypes are also set to null and frozen\\n- **`hardenRegExp(pattern)`**: Overrides all user-overridable RegExp methods (`[Symbol.match]`, `[Symbol.matchAll]`, `[Symbol.replace]`, `[Symbol.search]`, `[Symbol.split]`, `exec`, `flags`, etc.) with the original primordial versions, preventing poisoned RegExp objects from hijacking string operations\\n- **`{ __proto__: null, ...desc }` pattern**: Used pervasively when defining property descriptors to ensure descriptor objects themselves have no prototype chain\\n- **`ObjectSetPrototypeOf(primordials, null)` and `ObjectFreeze(primordials)`**: The entire primordials namespace has its prototype removed and is frozen at the end of the file\\n- **Safe Promise combinators**: `SafePromiseAll`, `SafePromiseAllSettled`, `SafePromiseAllReturnArrayLike`, `SafePromiseAllReturnVoid`, `SafePromiseAllSettledReturnVoid`, `SafePromiseAny`, `SafePromiseRace`, `SafePromisePrototypeFinally` — all wrap calls to avoid exposing `SafePromise` prototype to user-land\\n- **`SafeStringPrototypeSearch`** and **`SafeArrayPrototypePushApply`**: Utility functions that use primordials versions of underlying methods\\n\\n## 2. kEmptyObject and kEnumerableProperty (lib/internal/util.js)\\n- **`kEmptyObject = ObjectFreeze({ __proto__: null })`**: A reusable frozen empty object with no prototype, used as the safe default for options parameters throughout the codebase. Prevents `options.constructor`, `options.__proto__`, or `options.toString` from causing pollution when options are spread or iterated.\\n- **`kEnumerableProperty = { __proto__: null }; kEnumerableProperty.enumerable = true`**: A safe property descriptor object with no prototype\\n- **`encodingsMap = { __proto__: null }`**: Encoding lookup map without prototype\\n\\n## 3. ObjectPrototypeHasOwnProperty / ObjectHasOwn checks\\nThroughout lib/, the primordials alias `ObjectPrototypeHasOwnProperty` (equivalent to `Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty.call(obj, key)`) and `ObjectHasOwn` are used instead of `obj.hasOwnProperty(key)` to guard `for...in` loops and object property access:\\n- **lib/internal/freeze_intrinsics.js**: Guards property access when freezing all JS intrinsics to prevent __proto__ / constructor keys from interfering\\n- **lib/internal/modules/cjs/loader.js**: Guards module cache lookups; `Module._cache`, `Module._pathCache`, `Module._extensions` all use `{ __proto__: null }` to prevent key collisions with Object prototype\\n- **lib/internal/modules/esm/assert.js, get_format.js, resolve.js, translators.js, helpers.js, typescript.js**: ESM loader uses `ObjectPrototypeHasOwnProperty` when checking import attributes, protocol handlers, and package exports\\n- **lib/internal/http2/core.js and lib/internal/http2/compat.js**: HTTP/2 headers stored in `Object.create(null)` objects (explicitly noted as intentional for security vs HTTP/1); `ObjectHasOwn` guards header iteration\\n- **lib/_http_outgoing.js**: Uses `ObjectHasOwn` when iterating user-supplied HTTP/1 response headers\\n- **lib/internal/crypto/util.js, lib/internal/crypto/webidl.js**: Guards registered algorithm maps; uses `ObjectPrototypeIsPrototypeOf` for interface checks\\n- **lib/internal/source_map/source_map.js, lib/internal/process/promises.js, lib/internal/assert/assertion_error.js, lib/internal/encoding/single-byte.js, lib/internal/util/inspector.js**: Scattered safe property checks in utilities\\n- **lib/internal/util/parse_args/utils.js and parse_args.js**: `objectGetOwn` and `optionsGetOwn` helpers built on `ObjectHasOwn`\\n- **lib/internal/vm/module.js, lib/internal/tty.js, lib/cluster.js, lib/internal/cli_table.js**: Safe `for...in` iteration using `ObjectPrototypeHasOwnProperty`\\n\\n## 4. Object.create(null) / { __proto__: null } for Data Containers\\n- **lib/internal/modules/cjs/loader.js**: All Module caches use `{ __proto__: null }` to prevent `__proto__`, `constructor`, or `toString` keys from being treated as special\\n- **lib/quic.js**: Constants objects use `ObjectCreate(null, { __proto__: null, ... })` combined with `ObjectSeal` for tamper-proof constant maps\\n- **lib/internal/error_serdes.js**: `TryGetAllProperties` accumulates into `{ __proto__: null }` to avoid prototype chain interference\\n- **lib/internal/bootstrap/realm.js, lib/internal/bootstrap/node.js**: Bootstrap binding objects use `{ __proto__: null }` to safely receive native bindings\\n- **lib/internal/modules/esm/create_dynamic_module.js**: Module reflection objects (`exports`, `imports`) created with `{ __proto__: null }`\\n- **lib/internal/events/abort_listener.js**: Return objects use `{ __proto__: null }`\\n- **lib/internal/heap_utils.js, lib/internal/webstreams/queuingstrategies.js, lib/internal/perf/nodetiming.js, lib/internal/streams/lazy_transform.js, lib/internal/webstorage.js**: Inspect option objects and property descriptors use `{ __proto__: null }`\\n- **lib/internal/errors.js**: SystemError property definitions use `{ __proto__: null }` for descriptors\\n- **lib/internal/test_runner/reporter/**: Test reporter objects (junit.js, rerun.js, utils.js) and tests_stream.js emit event data objects with `{ __proto__: null }`\\n\\n## 5. ESLint Enforcement (tools/eslint-rules/prefer-primordials.js)\\nAn ESLint rule enforces that core modules use primordials instead of global builtins, preventing accidental use of mutable prototype methods like `Object.create`, `hasOwnProperty`, `Array.prototype.forEach`, etc. directly.\\n\\n## 6. Safe Collection Usage\\n`SafeMap` and `SafeSet` are used extensively in core modules (`lib/internal/trace_events_async_hooks.js`, `lib/internal/watch_mode/files_watcher.js`, `lib/internal/bootstrap/realm.js`, `lib/internal/fs/recursive_watch.js`, `lib/internal/perf/usertiming.js`, `lib/internal/console/constructor.js`, `lib/internal/modules/esm/translators.js`, `lib/internal/cluster/child.js`, `lib/internal/fs/glob.js`, etc.) to ensure that iteration and storage operations cannot be poisoned by user code overriding `Map.prototype[Symbol.iterator]` or `Set.prototype[Symbol.iterator]`.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
